# Hamnix STATUS — milestone log

The full milestone trajectory across three tracks: the bare-metal Hamnix
kernel (M-series), the Linux ABI compatibility track (L-series), and the
Linux userspace ABI track (U-series).

**Status legend:**
- **Done** — landed on `main` with a passing test.
- **Partial** — landed but a documented gap remains.
- **Diagnosis** — investigated, documented blocker, no code change.
- **Pending** — not yet started.

For the current end-state plus open blockers, see [README.md](README.md).
For docs/architecture spec, see [docs/architecture.md](docs/architecture.md).
For agent-orchestrated development workflow, see [README.md§Agent-orchestrated development](README.md#agent-orchestrated-development).

> **Current boot model (read this before the milestone log below).**
> There is **no pre-baked root disk image** anymore. The single install
> artifact is `build/hamnix-installer.img` (built by
> `scripts/build_installer_img.sh`) — an ESP-only **UEFI-only** GPT image
> whose kernel + embedded squashfs root are loaded entirely into RAM by
> firmware; the in-RAM installer then partitions the target's NVMe and
> writes a persistent **GPT + ESP + ext4 root**, then reboots off that
> disk alone. The installed system boots when UEFI launches the native
> PE/COFF stub off the NVMe ESP, which ELF-loads `\hamnix-kernel.elf`;
> the kernel finds the ext4 root via its `.hamnix-roots` sentinel, binds
> `#sysroot` at `/`, and ELF-loads `/init` off ext4. For VM testing,
> `scripts/build_installed_nvme.sh` runs that real installer path once
> into a golden disk `build/hamnix-installed.qcow2`, and feature tests
> boot a fresh copy via `scripts/_installed_boot.sh`. **There is no
> BIOS/legacy/CSM path, no GRUB, and no bootable ISO** —
> `scripts/build_iso.sh` is now a shim that delegates to
> `build_installer_img.sh`. The in-kernel cpio initramfs is retained for
> the developer `-kernel` test path and as the installer's in-RAM root.
> Many milestone rows below are date-stamped historical records of the
> earlier hybrid-ISO / baked-image model and are preserved as history,
> not current state.

---

## Status

| Milestone | Description | Status |
|-----------|-------------|--------|
| T27 | **Daily-driver campaign + USER QA flood #3 (2026-07-15) — "make an OS I can move into"** — a large multi-track push toward daily-driver usability, all shipped + independently verified. **Media:** audio plays in the OS (`56c9101c`, #321 — WAV decode + player + real non-silent tone captured off the HDA codec; MP3 planned) and **video plays** (`e0a7cf7f`+, #322 — Motion-JPEG player reusing the JPEG decoder + a CC0 self-generated test clip; disproved-and-fixed a latent kernel bug where the compositor SILENTLY DROPPED any image >1020px — `sys_write` 4KiB-bounce chunking vs a whole-buffer `_wsys_blit_parse`; now streaming-reassembled; proven via a headless on-device gate: `blit_ret==196624`). **Browser depth** (daily-driver campaign): DOM API completeness — querySelectorAll/classList/events/dataset (`554d8647`, #320) + a real DOM tree with traversal + true CSS combinators + pseudo-classes + uppercase tagName (`3ae58a4f`, #324). **Text handling, desktop-grade:** Notes+URL-bar migrated to the #315 substrate (`ebafee20`, #319), middle-mouse PRIMARY + double-click-word/triple-click-line (`98cbc930`, #328), terminal select-and-copy-an-error (`f621a6fc`, #323). **DE UX:** menu drag-and-drop now drops WHERE YOU RELEASE (panel or desktop, creating a real `.desktop`) — the disproof was subtle (compositor routes drag only to the window under the cursor, so the menu committed instantly with no drop coord; the RECEIVER must commit on its own release) (`801b3639`, #327); cursor tail shallower, calculator shows the running `5+5` formula, hamfm opens in `/home/live` (`d7dc32c3`+, #329); Google usable (`56f5f553`, #317). **Stability landmines:** a SILENT SPONTANEOUS REBOOT root-caused to a silent triple-fault — vector-8 #DF was on `IST=0` (ran on the wrecked stack) on production boots; flipped it to the already-seeded per-CPU #DF IST stack, always-on, so a #DF now logs a trap frame instead of resetting the box (`eae4d35c`, #326). **CI** "continuously failing" disproved as runner-starvation (0 self-hosted runners; all GitHub-hosted) — it was a missing concurrency group + a too-fast push cadence; added a ref-scoped cancel-in-progress group (`67a04696`, #325). Verification lessons hardened into memory this wave: `/dev/mouse` injection is flaky, the host preview draws MONOSPACE and lies about proportional text positions (fooled the orchestrator into a wrong #328 send-back), the stale-image trap, and isolated-objdiff. Residuals filed (not dropped): intermittent menu distortion (devwsys geometry race, #330), host-preview-proportional infra fix (#331), MP3/H264/AVI/A-V-sync media follow-ups. **Both filed residuals since CLOSED:** #331 (`4f9876b7`) made `lib/hamui_host` render proportional (device-faithful; the ~10-monospace-assertion premise DISPROVED — every render gate asserts stable UI chrome, never glyph ink, so 0 assertion changes needed), and #330 (`1b277010`) fixed the menu shear — root-caused to a per-window cache **stride race**: the `geometry`/`parent` ctl verbs flipped `wsys_win_w` WITHOUT `wsys_present_lock`, so on SMP a width change between another CPU's rasterize and blit wrote the cache at the old (320) stride and read it at the grown-menu stride → every row drifts right (the sheared, shifted-right menu); plus a stale-slot leak (`wsys_alloc_wid` didn't reset geo/scene fields). Fix commits both writes under the present lock + resets slot geometry on alloc + a deterministic `wsys_geom_reset` boot selftest. Verified: `build_user`+`native_kernel_links` (ship blocker) green, `test_de_multiwin_taskbar` booted the DE and passed taskbar-churn/multitask/raise-enum (the exact slot alloc/free/realloc path) with no deadlock. Isolation param silently no-op'd again (agent correctly branched, not committed to main). **Follow-on autonomous stretch (2026-07-15, standing daily-driver campaign):** browser DOM rounds 3-6 + a native MP3 decoder, each host-iterated and orchestrator-verified before merge. #321-follow **MP3** (`cd25e74b`): native MPEG-1 Layer III decoder (`lib/mp3decode.ad` — bit reservoir, Huffman, IMDCT, polyphase synthesis; no libm) + player routing + a CC0 test `.mp3` in the image; host golden-vector gate proves a REAL decode (correlation **1.000000** vs ffmpeg, RMS within 1%), not a stub. **Browser round 3** (`17f2d992`): node identity (nodeType/nodeName/nodeValue), replaceChild + live childNodes sync, `:nth-child(An+b)`. **Round 4** (`0d607233`): `.innerHTML` SETTER parses fragments into real queryable child nodes (via a default-OFF jsengine member-set seam — pure-JS path proven inert by the jsengine gates) + the filed #250 CSS multi-line-property bug. **Round 5** (`1dd97bbe`): `querySelector`/`getElementById`/getElementsBy* now traverse the created-node tree (createElement/appendChild + innerHTML nodes), with source↔created crossover for descendant/child combinators. **Round 6** (`afc9daea`): the round-5-surfaced correctness bug — the source-text selector scanner walked `<script>`/`<style>` bodies, so markup in a JS string literal was falsely matched; now skips raw-text-element bodies per HTML CDATA rules. **Round 7** (`90ee324d`): `element.style` manipulation — DISPROVED the premise (round 4 already gave every element a live `.style` object flowing into the inline-style cascade with `display:none` layout drop); closed the real gaps — `.style.width`, `.style.cssText`, and made `setAttribute('style',…)`/`getAttribute` share the SAME store as `.style` (was a latent clobber bug), plus fixed a heap-move dangling-pointer in the cssText parser. **Round 8** (`8a19265d`): event dispatch that actually FIRES — DISPROVED the premise (dispatchEvent/preventDefault/the Event object already worked); the real gaps were a single-listener slot (addEventListener + onclick overwrote each other), no bubbling, a no-op stopPropagation, no currentTarget. Now a multi-listener registry fires all handlers in registration order + the attribute handler, bubbles target→ancestors with working stopPropagation/currentTarget, and a real pointer click shares the same dispatch core; a handler's DOM mutation re-renders. **Round 9** (`9692d030`): form submission — DISPROVED the premise (input.value get/set, checkbox/radio/select serialization, `el.name`/`type` props already worked); the real gaps were the JS `form.submit()` method (entirely absent) and making the `submit` event bubble/cancelable. Now `form.submit()` GET-serializes named controls (URL-encoded) → `action?k=v...` navigation, and a `submit` listener calling `preventDefault()` blocks navigation (the key SPA behavior), riding round 8's dispatch core. **Round 10** (`852710cb`): CSS positioning — partial disproof (relative/absolute + top/left/right/bottom already parsed & relocated TEXT segments; `fixed`→absolute mapped); the real gaps were `z-index` (unparsed, no stacking), **background-fill** relocation (only text moved, not the box's background rect), and no gate. Now z-index flows through the cascade (stylesheet + inline/`​.style`), positioned boxes relocate their background fills by the same delta as text, and `lib/htmlpage.ad` paints element backgrounds in a stable z-index sort (z==0 pages byte-identical). Coverage: relative/absolute/fixed + top/left + z-index + nearest-positioned-ancestor containing block; deferred: sticky, dedicated right/bottom gating, text z-ordering, stacking contexts beyond a flat z-sort. Each round: `build_user` rc=0 + full hambrowse host suite green (now 24 gates; agent ran 27/27 incl. gfx/cascade/extcss) + jsengine gates green where touched. Net across rounds 3-10 the engine went from static-render to genuinely interactive: real DOM tree, dynamic node create/query/mutate, innerHTML, correct selector scoping, element.style, firing/bubbling events, form submission, and CSS positioning. **Round 11** (`6349e4a9`) — an EMPIRICAL real-site compat AUDIT (render 3 realistic fixtures — marketing/flex, full form, JS SPA — catalogue what breaks): produced `docs/hambrowse_compat_audit_2026-07-15.md` (prioritized, repro-backed) + fixed 2 found bugs (a spurious `border-radius` 1px frame from a `border` prefix-match; dropped `rgba()` colours). Disproved the pessimistic premise — the JS DOM stack is genuinely strong (querySelectorAll/dataset/classList/createElement/appendChild/Array methods/addEventListener+dispatch all work). This rotated the campaign from guessing features to evidence-steered. **Round 12** (`efe42d89`) — fixed the audit's #1 (page-breaking) finding: `innerHTML=''`/reassignment now DETACHES prior JS-created children (was leaving the created-node `ap_*`/`cc_*` render edges linked → a re-rendering SPA doubled content: 7 lines for 4 tasks); proven by a double-render gate asserting exactly 4 rendered rows. Bundled `list-style:none` + `text-decoration:line-through` parse. Surfaced a distinct follow-up (deliberately not forced): `<li>` elements bypass the class cascade entirely (`_open_style` skipped), so a `.done` list item's colour/strike never applies — a dedicated round because unclosed `<li>` makes a naive per-li style push corrupt the stack. **Round 13** (`09b2a4e6`) — closed that follow-up: `<li>` now applies its own class/inline cascade (colour + strike + weight, same `_open_style` path as `<p>`/`<blockquote>`) so `<li class="done">` renders struck+greyed; leak-safe against unclosed `<li>` via a **synthesised implicit close** (idempotent `_li_close_lvl` per list level, fired at `</li>`, the next same-level `<li>`, and `</ul>`/`</ol>`), guarded to real list depths so a stray `<li>` can't push/OOB. Proven by an unclosed-`<li>` fixture (3 styled items, no strike/colour bleed into a trailing `<p>`) + the clearrebuild gate's assertion corrected to expect exactly 1 struck + 3 unstruck. All 27 host gates green incl. every flex/nav/list gate. **Round 14** (`cf5f3a14`) — audit finding #8 (flex items over-shrink, split words: "Nimbus"→"Nim"/"bus"). DISPROVED the audit's free-space-distribution suspicion: real cause is a **measure-unit mismatch** — flex tracks sized to a monospace `CELL_W` estimate at container-open, but text laid out with the PROPORTIONAL measure hook (device + gfx render-PNG driver), so a wide bold brand word overflows its too-narrow track and gets hard char-broken (invisible to the plain monospace host harness — only the gfx driver reproduces it). Fix: a min-content floor at the word-wrap layer — inside a flex item, suppress the single-word hard char-break (`g_flex_item_depth`) and treat content-sized items as nowrap (`g_flex_nowrap_depth`); both flags 0 off the flex path (zero-cost, normal prose wrapping untouched). Approximates the 90% (intact word overflows its track; no sibling-slack redistribution). 29/29 host gates green (new `flexmin` gate under the gfx driver). **Browser campaign checkpoint (rounds 3-14 + audit):** the page-breaking and major-degrade audit findings are all closed; remaining catalogue items are lower-severity (position:fixed right/bottom stretch, `<fieldset>` border) — cosmetic. Next daily-driver priorities to weigh over more browser polish: verify on-device MP3 HDA playback (decoder is host-golden-vector-verified only) and A/V-sync for the video player. **Two agents (rounds 8, 9) hit the known idle-wait-without-committing pathology ([[feedback_agent_must_commit]]) — caught both by inspecting the worktree branch directly and nudging; work was intact and recovered.** **Process lesson this stretch (memory-recorded):** the earlier "isolation silently failing" was operator error — the `isolation:"worktree"` PARAMETER was never passed (only stated in prompt text, which the `feedback_agent_isolation_param` memory explicitly warns does nothing); once passed as a real param, worktrees are created and confirmed via `git worktree list` before trusting isolation. | **Done** |

| T24 | **Adder language roadmap + std-lib foundation (autonomous track) + DE first-boot hardening** — a run of byte-lockstep, byte-inert-when-unused Adder increments toward "best systems+app language" (detail in `docs/adder_language_roadmap.md`): sum types + `Option`/`Result` + `?` + exhaustive `match` (seed+native), opt-in null-safety `!`, descriptive traps + `@unsafe`/pragma, `Slice[T]` fat pointers, `Own[T]` move-only affine, default+keyword args. Then a **std-lib foundation**: fixed the `cast[Ptr[T]](array_local)` seed↔native divergence (#296, now a permanent objdiff-corpus gate — native was value-loading where the seed leaq-decays an aggregate local); a seed-first `String` VIEW type `{ptr,len}` + `lib/strview.ad` helpers (#299 — the agent DISPROVED a heap-backed premise: no userland allocator existed); a real **userland heap allocator** `lib/hamalloc.ad` over `sys_mmap` (#300 — segregated free-lists, 14 size classes, arena growth, 16 B magic-guarded headers; 20 k-cycle churn stress-verified on-device, footprint bounded) **plus owning heap strings**. All: objdiff 256-accepted/0-diverged, fuzz 500/500, `native_kernel_links` (ship blocker) PASS, `build_user` PASS, per-increment on-device gates PASS, bench binaries md5-identical (1.83×-of-gcc-O2 held), byte-inert-off proven by md5. DE: **#288 first-boot scene-client hardening** — `hamdesktop`/`hampanelscene` were fire-and-forget with `exit(1)`-on-first-handshake-failure; added a bounded `sys_yield`-paced retry (no-op on the happy path), orchestrator boot-verified full desktop on a fresh image (residual: real-HW retest to confirm the intermittent cold-boot failure is gone). Kernel structurally exempt throughout (opt-out sacred). | **Partial (roadmap ongoing: regions + native String port remain)** |

| T9 | **DE OOM/panel fix (user-reported)** — every hamui app baked 8.2 MB of static framebuffer BSS; the ELF loader eagerly contiguous-allocated it per app → `elf: OOM` crash + no panel under `-m 1G`. Fixed by demand-paging the ELF64 BSS tail (`fs/elf.ad`) + right-sizing hamui backbuffers to the actual window via demand-zero mmap (`lib/hamui.ad`, ~8 MB→<1 MB/app). Crash + panel fixed, VISUALLY verified 3 boots. (Residual: desktop-icons/cursor-ghost flaky under extreme host load.) | **Done** |
| T10 | **SMAP/SMEP kernel-image protection** — the kernel high-half (.text/.rodata/.data/.bss + module window) was stamped US=1 (CPL3-readable) and the US=0 restamp was gated on `smap_supported` (never ran on non-KVM). Now unconditional US=0 restamp at the creation layer + US=0 module map; audit reports 0 high-half US=1 leaks; SMAP-enforcement test (user read of kernel VA faults) PASS. Unblocks KASLR/KPTI. | **Done** |
| T11 | **DE live-image OOM regression FIX (user-reported, orchestrator-VISUALLY-verified)** — the default installer image's in-RAM live distro had grown to **361 MiB** (the full real-Debian apt/dpkg closure was staged into the RAM image by default), but only ~316 MiB is free under the user's `-m 1G` ship command → `[live-root] memblock_alloc(378535936) failed`, the rootfs half-loaded, and the DE OOM'd spawning apps (bare teal desktop). Fix: the live in-RAM distro now defaults to a **minimal busybox namespace** (`HAMNIX_LIVE_MINIMAL`, build_rootfs_img.py / build_installer_img.sh) — 361→55 MiB; the heavy apt closure moves to the persistent installed disk / opt-in flag (apt-e2e image sets `HAMNIX_LIVE_MINIMAL=0`). Full desktop (panel + 3 app windows) boots clean at `-m 1G`, 0 OOM — orchestrator viewed the screendump. (Supersedes the T9 hamui-backbuffer fix, which is in-tree but was not the live-image regression.) | **Done** |
| T15 | **Linux-namespace apt/dpkg KEYSTONE — `dpkg -i` completes** — the fork+exec COW-isolation bug is fixed (`_cow_share_one_page` refcounts verbatim-RO shared mmap frames so a child's exec/reap teardown no longer frees a frame the parent still maps) + a cascade of install-pipeline ABI fills (rmdir/rename/lseek-ESPIPE/utimensat/O_TRUNC/*at-anchoring/binfmt_script/EFER.NXE-per-CPU). `dpkg -i` now reaches "Setting up hamhello" + the installed binary runs; all 3 gates (apt-e2e, heartbeat, dynamic_forkexec) green. `enter linux {sh}` is interactive over a real Debian root. | **Done** |
| T17 | **DE memory footprint −21 MiB + hamsh lexer truncation fix** — hamUId compositor BSS 40→20 MiB (DMAX 32→12, SCENE_CACHE right-sized, wallpaper buffers demand-mmap'd); DE boots full (panel+apps) with ~372 MiB free of 842 under `-m 1G`, zero OOM (orchestrator-VISUALLY verified). CRITICAL latent fix: hamsh's lexer silently truncated past `TOK_MAX=512`, so once `rc.5` grew past it the script truncated → parse error → BLANK desktop; now `TOK_MAX=4096` + all 6 token arrays resized + loud overflow error + CI guards (`test_hamsh_tok_capacity.sh`). Heartbeat green (clean host). | **Done** |
| T20 | **DE-OOM regression FIX + user-reported bug wave** — (1) a coverage agent un-gated-embedded ~120 Debian binaries into the DEFAULT installer cpio, bloating it 214→297 MiB → DE OOM on `-m 1G` (blank/partial desktop). Gated behind `HAMNIX_DEBIAN_BREADTH`; image back to 216 MiB; added `test_installer_img_size.sh` (fail >260 MiB) as a RAM-independent bloat tripwire; DE-tests default to 2G RAM (`HAMNIX_VM_MEM`). (2) A userspace process fault (the user's `ls \| grep`) was HALTING the kernel via the ring3-bringup trap-diag handler — now a CPL3 read-prot #PF delivers SIGSEGV+coredump+reap and the kernel keeps running (`test_user_fault_survivable` PASS). (3) hamedit Ctrl-S now persists saves + surfaces read-only write failures honestly. (4) Ops: reclaimed ~321 GB by pruning 1060 stale agent worktrees. All orchestrator-VISUALLY verified (full desktop at -m 1G, 216 MiB). | **Done** |
| T18b | **Optimizer — regalloc on the IR (scratch-register pool)** — the IR emit path now parks binop operands in callee-saved scratch registers (drawn from the linear-scan pool not claimed by a promoted local, provably disjoint, call-crossing-safe) instead of `%rbp` stack slots: 7→0 push/pop pairs on the register-pressure benchmark. RESIDUAL (#2 still open, with a CONCRETE diagnosis candidate): the underlying T24 GOT/reloc wrong-VALUE root cause is a STALE COW-shared `.got.plt` surviving image replacement. On the fork+exec path, `do_execve` (arch/x86/kernel/syscall.ad:2170 `vma_clear` + :2317-2324 `task_free_owner_regions`) deliberately does NOT free the old ELF-image pages — the comment at syscall.ad:2164-2166 states "the actual ELF-image pages... leak across execve" and :2317-2323 notes a fork+exec child COW-shares the parent image (`image_phys==0`) and is "left untouched". So the child keeps the PARENT's `.got.plt` mapped (GOT[1]=parent's `link_map`, GOT[2]=parent's `_dl_runtime_resolve`, both at the parent's interp bias) while the NEW image loads at a FRESH per-exec ASLR bias (syscall.ad:2195-2199). Lazy resolution then runs `_dl_runtime_resolve` via a stale GOT[2]/link_map at the wrong bias → resolved target in r11 is garbage/non-canonical → the apt `jmp *r11` #GP. NOT YET REPRODUCED in-worktree: the `lazyplt_fork` fixture needs `/lib64/ld-linux-x86-64.so.2` from the (unstaged) debian-minbase rootfs to load ld.so — same precondition as `test_dynamic_forkexec` (both SKIP here). Fix layer = execve image-teardown / GOT re-init on image replace (NOT a mm/vma page-stamp), to be verified once the rootfs is staged. | **Partial** |

(3) **Optimizer correctness fix** (`142fbac0`): the miscompile was a **regalloc live-range bug in `cfg.ad`** (`bb_new` snapshotted `bb_first` at block CREATION; a `while` exit/join block fills AFTER the body lowers → range truncated → linear-scan reused the carried value’s register → clobber). (4) **div/mod-by-const strength reduction** (`22165e5e`): pow2 + Granlund–Montgomery magic (signed+unsigned, edge-exact), `ADDER_OPT`-gated; flag-OFF byte-identical; flag-ON **1500/1500 fuzzer 0 miscompiles**; 480-prog guard bit-exact. **Bench ON-vs-C-O2 7.14×→5.70×**, ON/OFF 1.05×→1.19×, collatz 2.63× (beats C-O0). NEXT: instruction selection (LEA+load-fold+kill push/pop temp stack, `#477` in flight); ≤2× on every kernel likely needs a fuller instr-sel IR. (Filed `#478` hamfmscene native-vs-seed objdiff, `#479` stale-codegen-dump cache.) | **Done (round 1; ≤2× in progress)** |

| T36 | **Compiler-perf Phase 4: alu-load memory-source operand fold** (`7b2a68e2`, #480, `--opt`-gated, flag-OFF byte-identical). An 8-byte array element `arr[i]` used as an integer ALU source operand (ADD/SUB/MUL/AND/OR/XOR + 6 compares) is sourced in-place via `op (%rcx),%rax` (address from the existing scaled-index `lea`) instead of a separate load-to-temp; the register operand is held on the **stack** so the fold fires under register pressure + on nested binops. Commutative ops fold either side; SUB/directional-compares fold RHS only. **Sub-8-byte elements intentionally NOT folded** (a memory-source op is a full 64-bit fetch with no sign/zero-extension — correctness guard, negative-tested). | T41 | **Self-hosting integrity: fixed a real native miscompile — global Ptr[signed-subword] element load not sign-extended** (`33924f97`, #478). The lone persistent native-vs-seed objdiff divergence (`hamfmscene`) was NOT a benign encoding diff: `index_elem_signed()` in `codegen.ad` resolved pointee signedness for LOCAL/param `Ptr[T]` bases but had no GLOBAL `Ptr[T]` branch -> fell through to zero-extend, so the native build emitted `mov (%rax),%eax` where the seed emits `movslq (%rax),%rax` for a global `Ptr[int32]` element load. | T42 | **Build-hygiene: cached `ad_codegen_dump` auto-invalidates on compiler-source change** (`f09e5fb5`, #479). | T43 | **Compiler-perf P2 (gap-anatomy roadmap): real DCE + dead-store elimination — first lever to move the geomean** (`160414a5`, #485, `--opt`, flag-OFF byte-identical). `docs/perf_2x_roadmap.md` (#484) proved the ~5.4x gap is stack-machine codegen quality (not SIMD) and named P2 (delete dead defs+stores) as highest-ROI-fits-current-IR. | T45 | **Compiler-perf P1-lite (roadmap keystone): caller-saved IR scratch for call-free binop trees — kills push/pop** (`729bde67`, #487, `--opt`, flag-OFF byte-identical). The gap-anatomy named the value-at-a-time stack machine as the dominant residual. This extends the `--opt` IR scratch pool (`gen_expr_ir`) with a caller-saved extension `{rdi,r8-r11}` usable across any **call-free** IR tree — supplying registers when the callee-saved pool `{rbx,r12-r15}` is emptied by regalloc in pressured functions (matmul's promoted IVs), so inner-loop binop trees lower register-to-register instead of push/pop. Soundness: a scratch holds an operand only across ONE pure subtree, and a tree that re-emits a call refuses caller-saved scratch (safe regardless of whether the function calls elsewhere). **matmul inner-loop push/pop 124->68, 37 caller-saved scratch ops (was 0).** Verify: objdiff **213/213**, kobjdiff **10275/10275**; fuzzer **1100 programs 0 miscompiles** (deep nested trees + reg-pressure + eval-order/clobber probe); guard `test_opt_reglower` PASS (clean-cache, scratch fires + eval-order preserved). **Bench: matmul ON-vs-C-O2 6.93x->5.50x (~21%), geomean ON/OFF 1.24x->1.34x** (licm/collatz/saxpy also improved). | T46 | **Compiler-perf P1-cont: register-promote loop-carried IVs (fix cfg use-vector truncation)** (`2413d332`, #488, `--opt`, flag-OFF byte-identical). | T60 | **Kernel: detached-zombie address-space leak → fork-EAGAIN (USER-REPORTED bug-wave)** (`334517fa`). | T64 | **Kernel: fix task-slot double-free that intermittently broke DE boot** (`73f6ecbd`, QA campaign — found chasing the rc.5 partial-DE race; the namespace-probe theory was DISPROVEN). Symptom: a nondeterministic subset of the ~6 DE scene clients died at boot with `hamsh: command not found: /bin/hamX`, sometimes no panel/apps at all. ROOT CAUSE (kernel concurrency, latent since the detached/orphan reaps run on EVERY fork — T60/T62/T63 made it hotter): `task_reap` RCU-defers the slot's `STATE_FREE` publish but left it `STATE_EXITED` during the grace window; `reap_orphan_zombies()` (every fork) rescans `STATE_EXITED`, so during the DE fork burst a slot got **re-reaped before its RCU callback fired** → each re-reap queued another `call_rcu` that pushed the **same slot onto the freelist twice** → the intrusive O(1) freelist cross-links into a cycle → `free_head` collapses to FL_NIL while ~485 slots are genuinely free → `create_user_task: no free task slot` → `spawn`→-1 → "command not found". Census at failure was decisive (free=485, free_head=FL_NIL, ~9 double-pushes). FIX: new `STATE_REAPING` state — `task_reap` moves the slot there (not `STATE_EXITED`) before `call_rcu` + a **reap-once guard** (no-op on any non-EXITED slot) so a slot is reaped exactly once / pushed once; RCU callback gains the matching guard; `freelist_lock` (IRQ-masked) serialises pop/push/init vs the timer-IRQ RCU-callback push (a separate SMP race); `_state_label` maps REAPING→'Z'. Verify: **5/5 clean boots** (zero "no free task slot" / "command not found", all 6 scene clients up), full-DE screendump, `test_hamsh_heartbeat` PASS, new gate `test_de_slot_exhaustion.sh` (3/3). rc.5 + hamsh `_path_execable` needed NO change. | **Done** |

| T66 | **Kernel: serialise SMP UART RX drain — fix stray-NUL/`?` serial input corruption (QA item #8) + end-to-end Linux-ns shell PASS** (`13ca6168`). The serial shell (BOTH native hamsh AND `enter linux {sh}`) prepended a stray `?` to ~every-other command (`ls\|grep cat`→`?ls: not found`). ROOT CAUSE: a triple-drainer race on the 16550 RBR — the COM1 RX IRQ (`irq.ad` vec 36) AND the 100 Hz timer ISR on EVERY CPU (`time.ad`) both run `while (LSR&DR): inb(RBR)` with no mutual exclusion. On `-smp 2` two interleave: CPU-A sees DR=1, CPU-B/RX-IRQ pops the byte + clears DR first, CPU-A's stale RBR read returns the empty-FIFO 0x00 → a phantom NUL into the SW RX ring → busybox renders it `?` → misframed command. | T69 | **Security investigation: `test_security` newshell/shadow asserts were STALE — NO auth bypass** (`1f726614`, test-only). After the T68 flood fix unmasked `test_security`'s assertions, 3 FAILed (`/etc/shadow missing live:$6$`, `newshell <bad-user> didn't error`, `newshell wrong-password not denied`), seemingly CONTRADICTING T67's `test_newshell_auth_elevation` PASS. ROOT CAUSE (verified — only the TEST changed, no auth-code touched): the serial console runs as **uid 1 (hostowner)**, and `newshell <hostowner>` from uid 1 correctly takes the **password-FREE self-elevation fast path** (you don't prove a secret to become who you already are — `builtin_newshell` Step 1.5 in `user/hamsh.ad`), so the test's fed "wrong password" just ran as a command → no auth-failed line → false FAIL. FIX: `test_security` now `setuid 1000` FIRST, then `newshell live` (uid1000→uid1) prompts → wrong password → `/dev/auth` rejects → "authentication failed"; + corrected shadow/passwd field expectations for the 7-field format (T67). **CONCLUSION — NO auth bypass; auth path sound:** the seeded `etc/passwd` is correct (`live:x:1:1::/home/live:/bin/hamsh`, proper 7-field) and `etc/shadow` has the `live` hash; the real wrong-password-denial gate `test_newshell_auth_elevation` PASSes (dave/uid-1000 → denied); auth CODE is unchanged. **HONEST CAVEAT (corrects an earlier over-claim):** `test_security.sh` itself is STILL RED on a clean run — it fails ALL FOUR lookups (`/etc/passwd missing live:x:1:1`, shadow-missing, newshell-bad-user, newshell-wrong-password) which is the signature of a FLAKY TEST DRIVER not reliably capturing serial command output (same class as `test_fork_eagain` before its banner-gating hardening — NOT a product/auth defect, since the source files are correct and the auth gate passes). The `1f726614` assertion update is a partial improvement but the driver needs a proper hardening pass (re-send gated on a prompt/banner marker) to go green; deferred as test-infra, not security. | **Done (no-bypass VERIFIED; test_security driver hardening deferred)** |
| T70 | **SSH both ways QA: fix user-stack-overflow crash + exec round-trip — outbound/self-loop/sshd-session WORKING** (`18f36e11`, QA campaign item #9). The native SSH-2.0 stack (`user/ssh.ad` client + `user/sshd.ad` server: curve25519 KEX, ecdsa-p256 host key, chacha20-poly1305, password/pubkey auth) existed but was broken end-to-end. Two real bugs: (1) **CRITICAL user-stack overflow** — both files declared ~8 KiB packet buffers (`body[8200]`, `ct`/`plain`[8260], `macbuf`) as STACK locals, but the native user stack is a single 4 KiB page → the first ~8240-byte KEX frame faulted the guard page (write SIGSEGV) and the coredump/teardown took the KERNEL down; fixed by hoisting them to module BSS (matches the files' own "sizable buffers are top-level BSS" rule). (2) **`ssh host <cmd>` never ran** — sshd wired hamsh stdio via legacy dup2 int-fds, but hamsh's getty-flush skip-test queries the `/fd/0` NAME (stayed "cons" since SYS_SPAWN auto-populate was retired) → the flush drained+discarded the exec command from the pipe; fixed by Plan-9 stdio wiring (`sys_pipechan`+`SPAWN_STDIO_NS`+`sys_fdbind` of child `/fd/0=PIPE_R`,`/fd/1,2=PIPE_W`; sshd binds `/fd→#d`). **Outbound + self-loop + sshd-served session WORKING**: `test_ssh_loopback` PASS ×2 (full KEX + password auth + channel + `exec` sentinel round-trip over the encrypted channel; also made the client selftest self-validating — was a false-positive). heartbeat PASS. DEFERRED: inbound from host OpenSSH over SLIRP (`test_sshd`) still times out at banner — guest TCP reaches ESTABLISHED but userland `net_accept` never surfaces the connection = a pre-existing TCP-accept-handoff bug in the net layer, orthogonal to the SSH protocol code. | **Done (outbound/self/sshd-session; inbound net_accept deferred)** |
| T71 | **Kernel SMP: complete the `on_cpu` invariant — fix inbound-TCP-accept stack-corruption crash; inbound SSH TIER-3 working** (`d7cd352e`, QA campaign — found chasing the deferred inbound `net_accept` "handoff stall"). The stall was actually a **scheduler steal-window race that crashed the kernel on `-smp 2`** (#413 class, now properly closed): the `on_cpu` fence was raised only TRANSIENTLY inside `schedule()` just before `__switch_to_asm`, and the FIRST user task (`enter_first_task_sysret` — `sshd`/`u_server` in these tests) never raised it at all. So when that task set `STATE_WAIT` in `tcp_accept` + called `schedule()` but hadn't yet saved its `sp`, a wakeup on the other CPU flipped it READY and `_pick_next` (which didn't check `on_cpu`) dispatched it on the stale `sp` → **two CPUs executing one task on one kernel stack** → `__stack_chk_fail` + corrupted-return `#UD`. FIX (`kernel/sched/core.ad`): adopt the full Linux invariant — `on_cpu==1` for the ENTIRE time a task is a CPU's live task, cleared only by `__switch_to_asm` after it commits `prev->sp`; raise it at EVERY dispatch site (schedule main path, AP-idle dispatch, `sched_ap_launch`, the first-user-task sysret path); `_pick_next` + `_sched_try_pull_locked` skip `on_cpu!=0` (no waker-side spin — the waker can sit above the sleeping task on the same stack, which self-deadlocks). + independent latent fix (`drivers/net/virtio_net.ad`): `_virtio_net_drain_budget` did an unlocked RMW of the RX used ring (on-demand poll vs NAPI softirq on two CPUs) — serialized with a non-blocking `trylock`. VERIFIED `-smp 2`: **`test_sshd` PASS at TIER 3 (full interactive INBOUND ssh: connect → `uname` → output returns over the channel)**, `test_u_server`, `test_hamsh_heartbeat`, `test_smp`, `test_smp_soak` (80-kthread churn), `test_net_tcp` all PASS; the `smp_user` cpu1-affinity assertion failure is PRE-EXISTING (identical on baseline). **Unblocks ALL inbound-connection services** (inbound SSH now works; the native web engine #4 uses the same accept path). | **Done** |
| T72 | **Native web engine QA: serving WORKS (host a website) + fix virtio-net TX body-drop race; rendering is a gap** (`316fcff8`, QA campaign item #4). `user/httpd.ad` (accept loop) + `user/httpd_worker.ad` (per-conn workers, name-vhosts, static files+Content-Type, dir index, 404/403, CGI) is a real HTTP/1.1 server over Plan-9 `/net`; a **host-side fetch over QEMU SLIRP `hostfwd` now round-trips** (200 + full HTML body, 404, 403, correct Content-Type/Length). The serve path — freshly unblocked by the T71 inbound-accept fix — exposed a **virtio-net TX race**: `virtio_net_tx` reused ONE shared `vnet_tx_buf` + descriptor slot 0 per frame with no completion/reclaim, so an HTTP response's body segment overwrote the shared buffer while the device was still DMA-reading the header → **body silently dropped → connection hung** (`tcp_send` ACK-wait never advances; jiffies frozen in the IRQ-masked syscall ctx so no timeout/retransmit). A debug printk between the sends masked it = pure-timing Heisenbug. FIX: `virtio_net_tx` now waits for the device to publish the descriptor in the TX used ring before returning (buffer safe to reuse; bounded by the free-running PIT, works IRQ-masked) + serializes build+publish+drain under `local_irq_save`+spinlock (also closes a latent cross-CPU two-worker race). Verify: `test_httpd` PASS (was failing — serve+fetch 200/404/403), `test_net_http` PASS (outbound not regressed), heartbeat PASS. **RENDERING DOES NOT EXIST** (no HTML/CSS engine or browser — `hamview` is PPM/BMP only; `drivers/net/http.ad` is the apt client) — a clear large separate gap, not a bug. DEFERRED (pre-existing): `test_httpd_concurrent` OOMs (each worker has a 256 KB `body_buf` BSS; 4 simultaneous spawns + the harness's 10× retry storm exhaust 256 MB) — needs body-buf streaming or a concurrent-spawn cap, not a net bug. | **Done (serving works; renderer is a gap)** |

| T83 | **Installer: plant `.hamnix-roots` sentinel so the installed disk boots off ext4 — the OS is now INSTALLABLE** (`9eda8c9d`). The long-suspected "#413-class installed-boot instability" (installed golden-disk/NVMe deterministically NX-exec-faults on first task at `va=0xffffffff8055b590`, pid exits 139, before the shell) was **MISDIAGNOSED as an SMP/kernel-mapping bug** — it was an INSTALLER bug. `va=…8055b590` = `user_demo_entry`, the kernel's baked DIAGNOSTIC FALLBACK first-task that runs only when it can't load a real `/init`; it's a kernel-high `.text` symbol never mapped user-executable → dispatching it ring-3 SMEP/exec-faults (symptom, not disease). Real chain (from the boot log): the installed ext4 root had **no `.hamnix-roots` sentinel** → `#sysroot` never registered → `kernel bind '#sysroot' / FAILED` → `/init not found in namespace` → fell back to `user_demo_entry` → NX fault. Live boots `/init` from cpio, so ONLY the installed ext4 path needed the sentinel (hence live-vs-installed specific). FIX (`user/install.ad`): after `hpm install`, write `.hamnix-roots` = `sysroot .` (the whole-partition named-root form — `_freeze_named_source` prepends nothing for `.`, so `#sysroot`/init → `/ext/init`, matching the installer's flat layout) via the same `<dev>/ctl install_file` verb; zero hpm/DB changes. VERIFIED (golden disk rebuilt from the real installer path): `.hamnix-roots` present at ext4 root (debugfs), boot parses `#sysroot -> .`, `bind '#sysroot' / OK`, `ELF-loading /init`, reaches **runlevel 5 + interactive hamsh**, `echo`/`ls /bin` respond, **zero NX-fault / zero code=139 / zero command-not-found**. Live `-kernel` heartbeat PASS (479 ticks, no regression). BONUS: `test_user_home_mount` now BOOTS + passes useradd/passwd/auth/home-isolation (A/B/F/H/J); residual SEPARATE gap: per-user home file server doesn't implement directory listing (`ls /home/alice` → "listdir failed") — follow-up track. | **Done** |
| T84 | **Per-user home wired end-to-end: `useradd` → login → mounted+listable+isolated `/home/<name>`** (`d9e39d74`, follow-up exposed by T83). The "readdir missing" premise was a MISDIAGNOSIS — the `#<name>` home server's readdir already worked; the home was **never actually mounted** in the session, + 3 adjacent bugs. Root causes/fixes: (1) **`/etc/users/` never shipped** — `build_packages.py` listed `etc/users` as an etc FILE but it's a DIRECTORY (`default.ns`), so it was silently skipped → the installed disk had no `/etc/users/`, so login had no per-user recipe AND `useradd` couldn't write `/etc/users/<name>.ns` → `#<name>` never bound at `/home/<name>`; now ships every `etc/users/*.ns`. (2) **`fs/vfs.ad vfs_mkdir()` had no `#<word>` named-root arm** → `mkdir` of any path under the installed `bind '#sysroot' /` returned `-EROFS`; added `_hash_named_mkdir`/`_mkdir_named_subpath` → `ext4_mkdir_live`. (3) **`useradd` uid allocation** used "highest≥1000+1" → on stock passwd (`nobody:65534`) handed uid 65535; fixed to lowest-free ≥1000. (4) **`/home` didn't exist** on the partition → hostowner `ls /home` "listdir failed"; `useradd` now creates `/home/<name>`. Verify (golden installed disk): `test_user_home_mount` **PASS all 13** (`ls /home/alice` lists, `ls '#alice'` lists, `ls /home`→`. .. alice`, `cd`→`/home/alice`, uid 1002, marker isolated from native /home, zero "listdir failed"), heartbeat PASS (120 ticks), `test_shared_passwd_regular_user` + `test_linux_ns_dac` PASS (isolation not weakened). Minor known gap (best-effort, not test-required): `useradd` skel dirs (`Desktop`/…) via bare-literal `#alice/Desktop` don't materialize — a `resolve_path` `#word/<leaf>` canonicalization follow-up. | **Done** |
| T85 | **MM: SMP-safe execve image-region allocation — close the concurrent-execve phys-reuse race** (`e38d8b9b`). ROOT CAUSE (diagnosed by 2 prior agents, forced `HTTPD_MAX_WORKERS=1`): the physical region every `execve` carves for its ELF image was global RMW state guarded ONLY by the local boot-CR3 + `local_irq_save` window — masks LOCAL-CPU IRQs, **zero cross-CPU exclusion**. Path: `fs/elf.ad`→`page_alloc.region_alloc` (per-size bucket free-list)→cold-miss `memblock_alloc` (per-region bump cursor). On `-smp 2`, two concurrent execves both read the same bucket head / bump cursor → **identical phys region handed to two address spaces** (observed both `0x0a849000`) → mutual corruption. FIX (mirrors the proven `_pa_buddy_lock` T21/T64 discipline): `_memblock_lock` (IRQ-off LEAF spinlock around the bump-cursor scan/advance — innermost, calls nothing that locks) + `_pa_region_lock` (spinlock around the whole `region_alloc`/`region_free` critical section, inside the existing IRQ-off + boot-CR3 window; never nested with buddy_lock; memblock cold-miss hits memblock's leaf lock → no deadlock). Evidence: concurrent httpd workers now load at DISJOINT phys (`0x0c8db000` vs `0x0e000000`) — no collision/corruption/trap. Broadly valuable: makes ALL concurrent execve SMP-safe (DE app launch, shell pipelines, apt), not just httpd. Gates: **kobjdiff PASS 0 divergences/10291** (self-hosting invariant intact — the mm/ change is byte-identical to seed), `test_smp`/`test_smp_soak` (80-kthread) PASS, heartbeat/test_httpd/test_net_http PASS. FOLLOW-UPS: (a) `HTTPD_MAX_WORKERS` STAYS 1 — the "TCP wedges under >1 worker" is a SEPARATE bug (native `/net` accept + TCP stack serialize every peer through one TCP slot: SYN→ESTABLISHED→TIME_WAIT before the next SYN; >1 worker regressed the concurrency assertion 4/4→2/4, no crash — a TCP-concurrency track, not the MM race). (b) a PRE-EXISTING `hamsh` native-vs-seed objdiff divergence on the base tree (NOT from this change — hamsh imports none of these files; likely from the heavy identity/echo/home hamsh.ad churn T73-T84) — self-hosting follow-up to investigate. | **Done** |
| T86 | **Self-hosting: the flagged `hamsh` objdiff divergence was a HARNESS false-positive (no compiler bug) — objdiff gate now deterministic** (`dfc2e90a`, `scripts/objdiff_normalize.py`). The "lone hamsh native-vs-seed divergence" multiple agents reported (T85 note) was NOT a miscompile — the native compiler's hamsh codegen (`spawn`/`run_one_command`/`sys_waitpid_nb`) is byte-identical to the seed. Two latent harness bugs, both newly TRIGGERED by the T73-T84 hamsh churn: (1) the harness dropped seed `sys_*` funcs by NAME prefix, but recent churn added `sys_waitpid_nb` — a genuine USER function (real `endbr64`, no `syscall`) — so the seed came up one function short (621 vs 622) → greedy matcher misaligned; (2) canary-owner mis-attribution: `seed_canary_funcs` matched the stack-protector label `.__epilogue_spawn_resolved` to the shorter `spawn` via loose substring in **PYTHONHASHSEED-dependent set order** → subtracted a mov-pair from the wrong histogram → phantom divergence (hence the hash-seed-dependent FLAPPING). FIX: drop a `sys_*` seed func only if it actually issues a `syscall` (shape-based, matching native's `is_wrapper`); pick the LONGEST (most-specific) canary-owner name (deterministic). Result: `test_native_vs_seed_objdiff` **213/213, 0 divergences, now STABLE across PYTHONHASHSEED 0/1/2/3/42** (was flapping 1-clean/2-diverged — itself a real integrity-gate non-determinism bug); kobjdiff PASS 0/10291; heartbeat PASS. No compiler change. | **Done** |
| T87 | **Exec: serialize `do_execve` image-load — complete concurrent-execve correctness; httpd MAX_WORKERS 1→4** (`f404c73c`). Chasing the "httpd concurrency wedge" (attributed to TCP), the agent PROVED **TCP was never the limiter**: the native `/net` accept path handles N concurrent connections fine (under the 4-client burst, slots 1-4 each independently SYN→ESTABLISHED→accepted; the #166 multi-listener backlog + 256-slot 4-tuple demux all work). REAL root cause = a concurrent-execve race in the LOADER (beyond T85's region-freelist lock): `do_execve` records the loaded image via SHARED GLOBAL result state (`elf_last_*` in `fs/elf.ad`) + stages path/argv/shebang in shared kernel BSS, written assuming one-task-at-a-time. With >1 worker execve-ing on `-smp 2`, two loads clobber each other's `elf_last_*` and both map+record the SAME `region_alloc`'d image phys (observed: pid 11 & 12 both `image phys=0x0a849000`) → one's `task_reap`→`region_free` frees a region the other still runs → cross-image corruption → silent full-guest wedge. T85 locked only the region free-list RMW, not this larger loader-global critical section. FIX: `do_execve` runs under a global `_execve_lock` spinlock (thin wrapper; inner releases on the success SYSRET path, wrapper on every error return; kernel-mode non-preemptible + SYSCALL masks IF → no self-deadlock / not IRQ-taken). execve isn't hot; connection SERVING (tcp recv/send) still fully overlaps — only the brief image load serializes. + `user/httpd.ad HTTPD_MAX_WORKERS` 1→4. Evidence: `test_httpd_concurrent` **concurrent_ok=4/4 CONCURRENCY_PASS** at 4 workers (was 2/4 wedge — bisected), kobjdiff PASS 0/10291, heartbeat/test_smp/test_httpd/test_sshd(tier-3) PASS. Completes concurrent-execve correctness (T85 was partial). | **Done** |
| T88 | **VFS: close `#t<word>` named-root mkdir collision** (`4fceadc1`). Follow-up to T84's useradd skel-dirs. The bare `#alice/Desktop` case already worked (T84's `_hash_named_mkdir`), but a real remainder: `vfs_mkdir`'s `#t` tmpfs-server fast-path (`fs/vfs.ad`) matched `name[1]=='t'` WITHOUT the `name[2]==0||'/'` guard that every other named-root site (`_spec_localize`, the `#r` cpio reader) uses. So a multi-char named root starting with `t` — a per-user home `#tom` (user "tom"), or `#tux`/`#tmp` — was captured by the `#t` arm → `tmpfs_mkdir("om/Desktop")` → parent-walk fails → **silent create drop** (the "skel dir never materialized" symptom, for t-prefixed names). mkdir thus diverged from open/read/stat (which localize through the guarded `_spec_localize`). FIX: add `and (name[2]==0 or name[2]==47)` to the `#t` mkdir arm; `#t`/`#t/...` still route to tmpfs, `#t<word>` falls through to `_hash_named_mkdir`→`ext4_mkdir_live`. New `vfs_named_mkdir_selftest` (boot-armed by `/etc/ext4-mkdir-test`) proves a `t`-prefixed named-root create lands on ext4 not tmpfs. Gates: `test_ext4_mkdir` PASS (`[ext4-mkdir]` + new `[vfs-named-mkdir]`), `test_native_vs_seed_kobjdiff` PASS 0/10293, heartbeat PASS (1395 ticks). Minimal; doesn't touch T84 bound-path or T82 root-listing. **Clears the tracked backlog.** | **Done** |
| | _(kobjdiff CORRECTION: the `vma_tree_selftest` divergence WAS **REAL**, not an artifact — orchestrator confirmed `test_native_vs_seed_kobjdiff.sh` FAILs on main (`KOBJDIFF_EXIT=1`): native vs seed differ in instruction mix (loadimm 117 vs 118, test 63 vs 65, xor 0 vs 1) for this one kernel fn's DEFAULT codegen. A self-hosting T41-invariant violation latent since `vma_tree_selftest` landed (#504). Earlier T57 "kobjdiff 0 divergences" was a MISREAD launcher exit code — withdrawn. | M16.93 | Phase B: Plan 9 syscall numbers reserved + SYS_ERRSTR (265). 9 new numbers stubbed (-ENOSYS): rfork (256), bind (257), mount (258), unmount (259), create (260), stat (261), fstat (262), remove (263), fd2path (264). SYS_ERRSTR has a real body in `sys/src/9/port/error.ad` with 9front-style swap-buffer semantics; reads the per-task `errstr_buf` (128 B inline in `TaskStruct`) into a user buffer, and if the user buffer carries a non-empty string, installs that as the new current error. Integrated at exactly one failure path (SYS_OPEN → -ENOENT installs "file does not exist") so `tests/test_errstr.ad` can round-trip the message end-to-end. Foundation for every following Plan 9 native syscall — they all need `errstr` to report errors. See `docs/architecture.md` (Phase B/C of the migration plan) and `docs/native-api.md` for the syscall contract | **Done** |
| M16.94 | Plan 9 `/dev/cons` device file — `vfs_open('/dev/cons')` (and the OWRITE variant) returns an `FD_CONS_MARK` fd whose read side blocks on the existing kbd/UART RX FIFOs and whose write side fans bytes through `early_putc()` to UART + VGA/fb + printk. First concrete Layer-1 cdev landing under `sys/src/9/port/devcons.ad`; mirrors 9front's `/sys/src/9/port/devcons.c` at minimum scope. | M16.95 | Plan 9 `/dev/time` + `/dev/pid` + `/dev/random` device files — three new stateless cdevs under `sys/src/9/port/devtime.ad`, `devpid.ad`, `devrandom.ad` with `FD_TIME_MARK` (0xFFFFFFF0) / `FD_PID_MARK` (0xFFFFFFEF) / `FD_RANDOM_MARK` (0xFFFFFFEE) plumbing in `fs/vfs.ad`. `/dev/time` reads emit `get_jiffies()*10_000_000` ns-since-boot as ASCII decimal + `\n` (HZ=100 → 10 ms per tick); `/dev/pid` reads emit `current_task_pid()` as ASCII decimal + `\n`; `/dev/random` reads stream xorshift64 bytes (lazy-seeded from `get_jiffies()` mixed with the golden-ratio constant on first read — placeholder pending chacha20 + RDRAND/RDSEED). Writes return -1 on time/pid; `/dev/random` XOR-folds writes into the PRNG state as entropy mix. Retires the `SYS_GET_JIFFIES → read("/dev/time")` and `SYS_GETPID → read("/dev/pid")` rows in the migration table. See `scripts/test_devtime.sh`, `scripts/test_devpid.sh`, `scripts/test_devrandom.sh` | **Done** |
| M16.96 | DHCP client + virtio_net_tx public surface + IPv4/UDP/ICMP scaffold (`drivers/net/dhcp.ad`, `drivers/net/ip.ad`, `drivers/net/udp.ad`, `drivers/net/icmp.ad`, `drivers/net/virtio_net.ad` +`virtio_net_tx`). `eth_tx()` now wires through to the TX virtqueue (replaces the M16.90 log-and-drop stub); `ip_send()` builds the 20-byte IPv4 header with Internet checksum and resolves dst MAC via the ARP cache (broadcast for `255.255.255.255`, gateway MAC for off-subnet). DHCP client runs the four-way DISCOVER → OFFER → REQUEST → ACK handshake against SLIRP, captures `10.0.2.15` + gateway `10.0.2.2`, and mirrors them into the IP layer + ARP responder. ICMP echo request/reply skeleton lands but the reply parse path is gated by an arp_lookup codegen quirk fixed in M16.97. See `scripts/test_net_dhcp.sh` | **Done** |
| M16.97 | ICMP echo round-trip — finishes the M16.96 scaffold. Root cause was two Adder codegen quirks in `arp_lookup`: (1) `cast[uint64](arp_ip[i])` on an `Array[N, uint32]` global doesn't zero-extend cleanly across `==`, so the equality compare reported "not equal" even when bit-patterns matched; (2) `&arp_mac[i][0]` on the 2-D `Array[N, Array[6, uint8]]` MAC table lowered to address 0 instead of the correct slot, so `ip_send` saw `dst_mac == NULL` and dropped every outbound IP frame. Workaround in `drivers/net/arp.ad`: load `arp_ip[i]` through an explicit `Ptr[uint32]` + mask, and offset off `&arp_mac` arithmetically (`mac_base + i*6`). Both quirks documented in `memory/feedback_compiler_quirks.md` for a future compiler milestone. With the fix, `[icmp] echo request -> 10.0.2.2` followed by `[icmp] echo reply from 10.0.2.2` round-trips through the SLIRP gateway — first proof of two-way IPv4 in the bare-metal kernel. See `scripts/test_net_icmp.sh` | **Done** |
| M16.98 | Phase C: Plan 9 `rfork(2)` (SYS_RFORK = 256) lands its real body in `sys/src/9/port/sysproc.ad`, replacing the M16.93 -ENOSYS stub. POSIX-fork combo `rfork(RFPROC \| RFFDG \| RFNAMEG \| RFENVG)` creates a new task that returns the child pid in the parent and 0 in the child; in-place mutation (no RFPROC) privatises the namespace via RFNAMEG / RFCNAMEG. `TaskStruct` grows three sharing-state fields (`fd_table_refcount`, `namespace_id`, `note_group`) with matching accessors + monotonic id allocators (`alloc_namespace_id` / `alloc_note_group_id`) in `kernel/sched/core.ad`. `user/runtime.S` adds a `sys_rfork(flags)` wrapper that stashes the parent's user-side `%rbp` into syscall arg a5 so `do_rfork` can patch the child's initial `__switch_to` stack image (without this the child's first RBP-relative local read after rfork lands on the parent's stack page). `RFMEM` (thread path) returns -ENOSYS in this commit — full thread route lands in a follow-up. SYS_CLONE (3) stays untouched for the Linux ABI; both work concurrently. See `scripts/test_rfork.sh` for the end-to-end fixture. Cornerstone of the Plan 9-shape process control surface — replaces fork / vfork / clone / pthread_create / unshare with one flag-bit primitive | **Done** |
| M16.99 | Minimal DNS resolver client (`drivers/net/dns.ad`) — UDP/53 A-record queries against the DHCP-supplied DNS server (option 6, captured by `dhcp_get_dns` added to `drivers/net/dhcp.ad`). `dns_lookup("example.com", out_ip, timeout)` is the synchronous entry point: it primes the ARP cache with a one-shot REQUEST for the DNS server (10.0.2.3 under SLIRP has its own MAC distinct from the gateway at 10.0.2.2, so the M16.88 probe doesn't cover it), builds a 12-byte header + length-prefixed QNAME + QTYPE=A/QCLASS=IN, sends from an ephemeral source port in the 53000..53003 pool, and polls `virtio_net_poll()` until `dns_rx` flips the slot to "answered" or the deadline elapses. Response parser walks past the question section (honoring 0xC0-0xC0 compression pointers) and scans the answer section for the first A-record's RDATA. 4-slot in-flight table dodges the M16.97 2-D-array-address codegen quirk by flattening per-slot result bytes into a 1-D `Array[16, uint8]`. `udp_rx` dispatches dst-port 53000..53003 → `dns_rx`. `[dns] resolved example.com -> 172.66.147.243` against QEMU SLIRP's DNS forwarder is the proof-of-life marker; test accepts `[dns] timeout` as a SKIP for sandboxed CI without internet. See `scripts/test_dns.sh`. Unblocks `apt update http://deb.debian.org` reaching real package mirrors by name | **Done** |
| M16.100 | PS/2 keyboard polish for real-hardware install console (`drivers/input/atkbd.ad`). Extends the M16.75 Set-1 scaffold with: extended-scancode handling via a sticky `in_e0_prefix` flag (arrow keys, Home/End, Insert/Delete, PageUp/Down, right Ctrl, right Alt/AltGr); modifier-state bitmask (`MOD_SHIFT`/`CTRL`/`ALT`/`CAPS`/`NUM`) driven by make/break for Shift/Ctrl/Alt and toggle-on-make-only for CapsLock/NumLock; Shift+letter and Caps+letter folded via XOR (both pressed cancels, matching every PC keyboard since 1985); Shift+symbol routed through a parallel `sc1_to_shifted` table (`1`→`!`, ``` ` ```→`~`, …, US-104 layout); Ctrl+letter folded to 0x01..0x1A via `& 0x1F` so Ctrl-C still produces 0x03 and the M16.42 SIGINT path keeps working; F1..F4 emit VT220 SS3 escapes (`ESC O P/Q/R/S`), F5..F12 + Insert/Delete/PageUp/PageDown emit `ESC [ <digits> ~`, arrows emit `ESC [ A/B/C/D`. Boot-time `atkbd_self_test()` feeds 12 synthetic scancode sequences through `atkbd_process_byte()` and asserts 25 FIFO bytes; banner `atkbd: self-test PASS (25 cases)` is the regression criterion in `scripts/test_atkbd_ext.sh`. | M16.101 | Phase C: Plan 9 file-operations cluster — `create` (260), `stat` (261), `fstat` (262), `remove` (263), `fd2path` (264) — real bodies in `sys/src/9/port/sysfile.ad`, replacing the M16.93 -ENOSYS stubs. `do_create` delegates to `vfs_open_write`; DMDIR returns -1 + errstr "create failed: DMDIR not supported" (no `vfs_mkdir` backend yet). `do_stat` walks the cpio archive and serialises a 9P-shape `Dir` record per `docs/native-api.md`'s "Directory format". `do_fstat` handles per-`FD_*_MARK` synthetic dirs (cons / time / pid / random / null / zero / stdin / stdout / stderr / dir / pipe) plus initramfs fds. `do_remove` is a thin `vfs_unlink` wrapper. `do_fd2path` returns canonical cpio name for initramfs fds (best-effort; per-fd path slot deferred to Phase G). `user/runtime.S` gains a generic `syscall6(nr, a0..a5)` trampoline. | M16.102 | Minimal TCP/IPv4 client (active-open only) in `drivers/net/tcp.ad` — fleshes out the M16.51 scaffold into a real state machine. 8-entry static TCB table (parallel arrays, slot-index = ephemeral-port-offset from 50000), states CLOSED → SYN_SENT → ESTABLISHED → FIN_WAIT_1/2 → TIME_WAIT → CLOSED (passive-open / LISTEN deferred until sshd needs it). Public API: `tcp_connect(ip4, port, timeout)` returns slot; `tcp_send(slot, buf, len)` writes one segment + polls for ACK; `tcp_recv(slot, buf, max, timeout)` polls until data lands; `tcp_close(slot)` runs the FIN/ACK/FIN/ACK termination. ISN xorshift64-seeded off `get_jiffies()`. Checksum builds the IPv4 pseudo-header (src_ip + dst_ip + 0 + proto=6 + tcp_length) into a scratch prefix before the segment and feeds the whole thing through `ip_csum16` — same algorithm UDP/ICMP use, just with a different prefix. `ip_rx` gains a `proto == 6` dispatch path to `tcp_rx`. **Real bug found**: `ip_rx` previously handed the L4 demuxer the full buffer length, so a 40-byte TCP-ACK delivered in a 60-byte Ethernet-padded frame looked like it carried 6 bytes of phantom payload, advancing `rcv_nxt` past the next real data and dropping the echo; the fix trusts the IPv4 `total_length` field (capped at buffer length to defend against spoofed sizes). On-link destinations are ARP-primed via a one-shot REQUEST before the SYN; off-link targets route via the M16.96 gateway MAC. Smoke test in `init/main.ad:tcp_smoke_test` opens to 10.0.2.100:7 (SLIRP `guestfwd=tcp:10.0.2.100:7-cmd:cat` echoes via the host's `cat`), sends `"hi\n"`, reads it back, closes. Markers `[tcp] connected slot=0` / `[tcp] sent 3 bytes` / `[tcp] received 3 bytes: 'hi\n'` / `[tcp] closed slot=0` are the PASS criteria. No retransmission, no congestion control beyond cwnd=1 segment, no SACK / timestamps / window scaling (all explicitly out of scope for SLIRP's loss-free virtual wire). Unblocks the HTTP client that `apt update` needs. See `scripts/test_net_tcp.sh` | **Done** |
| M16.103 | Bare-metal Intel e1000e Gigabit NIC driver (`drivers/net/e1000e.ad`) — second real NIC after M16.88 virtio-net. PCI vendor 0x8086 + class 0x02/0x00/0x00 match plus a device-ID whitelist covering 82574L (0x10D3 — what QEMU's `-device e1000e` emulates), 82583V (0x150C), 82573L (0x10F5), 82579LM (0x1502, Ibex Peak PCH), I217-LM (0x153A, Lynx Point), I218-LM (0x15A2, Wildcat Point), I219-LM (0x156F, Sunrise Point) + v3 (0x15B7, Skylake). MEM + bus-master enable, BAR0 (MMIO) map, CTRL.SLU+ASDE for PHY/link bring-up, MAC read from RAL[0]/RAH[0] (post-EEPROM, no EEPROM-walk dance), 256-descriptor RX ring (4 KiB page, 16 B/desc) with 256 × 2 KiB per-descriptor receive buffers, RDBAL/RDBAH/RDLEN/RDH/RDT wired, RCTL programmed for EN + BAM (broadcast accept) + BSIZE=2K + SECRC. `e1000e_poll()` walks descriptors `(rx_tail+1)..` checking `status.DD`, strips length, hands frames to `eth_rx`, re-arms each descriptor + advances RDT. Scope is PROBE + IDENTIFY + RECEIVE only — no TX, no integration with the ARP/IP/UDP/ICMP/DHCP/DNS/TCP stack. virtio-net stays the bring-up NIC for those tests; e1000e just proves Intel silicon is reachable. Polled (no IOAPIC yet); MSI-X + full TX + IRQ wiring are explicit follow-ups. With virtio-net + e1000e, the install ISO now talks on the wire on every Dell PowerEdge / HP ProLiant / Supermicro motherboard / ThinkPad / Latitude / EliteBook from the last ~15 years. See `scripts/test_net_e1000e.sh` | **Done** |
| M16.104 | Per-task brk — fixes glibc-malloc heap-grow crash. The U39 Python milestone needed `-X heapsize=64k` to dodge a `"brk adjusted to free malloc space"` SIGABRT inside glibc's arena bookkeeping. Root cause: the `brk` syscall used a single global `linux_brk` cursor backed by kmalloc, and the kmalloc backing fragmented at page granularity — glibc's brk-grow path wants contiguous virtual address space, not page-quantised chunks. Fix: per-task `brk_base` / `brk_end` / `brk_max` fields on `TaskStruct` (zero-init in `kthread_create` / `create_user_thread`); rewrites the `linux_u` brk handler to honour them via a lazy-grow path. Multi-process Linux binaries no longer collide on a global cursor. The `-X heapsize=64k` workaround is dropped from `scripts/test_u39_python.sh` — Python now runs with glibc's default 1 MiB heap. Regressions: all 14 still PASS | **Done** |
| M16.105 | Bare-metal Realtek r8169-family NIC driver (`drivers/net/r8169.ad`) — third real NIC after M16.88 virtio-net and M16.103 e1000e. PCI vendor 0x10EC + class 0x02/0x00 match with device-ID whitelist {0x8139 (RTL8139 — the only Realtek model in modern `qemu-system-x86_64 -device help`), 0x8136 (RTL810x Fast Ethernet variant), 0x8161 (RTL8111B), 0x8168 (RTL8168 / RTL8111 — the chip on most consumer ASUS/Gigabyte/MSI boards + ThinkPads + gaming laptops), 0x8169 (older Gigabit)}. RTL8139 bring-up is implemented end-to-end: BAR0 (PIO window, 16 ports) read, PCI IO + bus-master enable, CONFIG1 LWAKE clear via 9346CR-gated config-unlock, software reset (CMD.RST poll-until-clear), MAC read from IDR0..IDR5, 9708-byte circular RX buffer allocated via `alloc_pages(2)` (8 KiB ring + 16 wrap overhead + 1500 slack), RBSTART planted with the buffer's <4 GiB physical address, RCR programmed for accept-physical-match + accept-broadcast + WRAP + RBLEN=8K, CMD.RE flipped to enable the receiver. Gigabit IDs (0x8168 / 0x8169 / 0x8161) are logged but not driven — the MMIO + 16-descriptor-ring path is deferred to a follow-up. `r8169_poll()` drains the circular buffer: walks header (`u16 status | u16 length`), validates `RXH_ROK`, hands `length - 4` bytes (strip CRC) to `eth_rx`, advances the shadow read offset (4-byte aligned, mod 8 KiB), and writes `(offset - 16) & 0xFFFF` back to CAPR per the data-sheet's offset-by-16 quirk. Scope is PROBE + IDENTIFY + RECEIVE only — no TX, no ARP/IP/UDP/ICMP/DHCP/DNS/TCP integration. virtio-net stays the bring-up NIC; r8169 just proves Realtek silicon is reachable. Polled (no IOAPIC yet); MSI / MSI-X + full TX + Gigabit MMIO + IRQ wiring are explicit follow-ups. With virtio-net + e1000e (Intel) + r8169 (Realtek), the install ISO now detects a working NIC on essentially every consumer x86 box from ~2009 onwards. See `scripts/test_net_r8169.sh` | **Done** |

| M16.108 | Plan 9 `/proc/<pid>/<file>` device family — first per-process introspection surface promised by `docs/native-api.md`'s "Reserved well-known paths" table. | M16.109 | TCP retransmission + RFC 6298 RTO — adds per-TCB retransmission state to `drivers/net/tcp.ad`. RTT samples feed Karn's algorithm: `rttvar = (3*rttvar + \|srtt - rtt\|) / 4`, `srtt = (7*srtt + rtt) / 8`, `rto = srtt + 4*rttvar` floored at 100 ms; skip RTT sample when retries > 0. Polling loops (connect-wait, send-wait, recv-wait) check `now - last_send > rto` and retransmit with exponential backoff (max 5 retries before -ETIMEDOUT). `scripts/test_net_tcp_retrans.sh` uses three-layer evidence (QEMU SLIRP is loss-free by construction so retrans rarely fires naturally): static `strings(ELF)` must contain both retrans + timeout format strings (proving code path is reachable), plus the existing happy-path TCP regression must still pass. Robustness for lossy real-internet paths | **Done** |

| M16.112 | Real-hardware install + boot guide — `docs/REAL_HARDWARE.md`. | M16.117 | AHCI / NVMe / e1000e / r8169 IRQ wiring — extends the M16.113 IOAPIC + per-vector handler-registration template to the remaining 4 bare-metal device drivers. Per-driver IRQ vectors: AHCI=0x41, NVMe=0x42, e1000e=0x43, r8169=0x44 (virtio-net at 0x40 from M16.113). Each driver's init reads PCI INTERRUPT_PIN + INTERRUPT_LINE, programs the IOAPIC redirection entry, registers a `*_irq_handler()`. | M16.118 | AHCI + NVMe WRITE paths — closes the read-only gap on both bare-metal disk drivers. | M16.120 | UEFI handoff partial completion — GetMemoryMap + ExitBootServices. | M16.122 | **Phase C.5: distro-shape namespaces** — `/bin/distrorun <distro> <cmd> [args...]` ships. Privatises the calling task's namespace via `rfork(RFNAMEG)`, opens `/var/lib/distros/<distro>` as a Chan, calls `mount(srvfd, ...)` (records the SRV-kind binding — inert in Phase C, will become a real 9P client mount when hamwd lands Phase D), then `bind`s `/etc /usr /lib /var` onto `backing/{etc,usr,lib,var}` (Phase C workaround: bind's prefix matcher only honors `path/` or `path\0`, so a single `bind("/", ...)` wouldn't match subpaths), then re-`bind`s `/home /net /srv /dev /proc` onto themselves to preserve shared file servers, then execs the target. End-to-end: namespaced read of `/etc/debian_version` returns `12.0` from `tests/distros/testdistro/`; native reads of `/etc/os-release` before and after return `hamnix/0.1` — both demonstrate the namespace isolation works AND hamsh's namespace is unaffected. **Linux compat is now opt-in per-process via namespace shape, not a property of the OS.** Phase B reserved syscalls (rfork, bind, mount, unmount, errstr, …) all carry weight. | M16.123 | AHCI + NVMe register with the kernel block layer — drivers now expose themselves as `sd0` (AHCI) and `nvme0n1` (NVMe) via `kernel/block/blk.ad`'s existing `register_blockdev(name, capacity, ops, priv)` + `BlockDeviceOps` vtable (which carries both `read_sectors` and `write_sectors` slots). | M16.124 | UEFI single-binary merge — honest blocker diagnosis. The M16.111+M16.120 wave was structured around merging `efi_stub.S` + `hamnix-kernel.elf` into one hybrid (PE+multiboot1 at offset 0) so the stub could reach `_x86_start_after_loader`. This commit is that follow-up but the conclusion is honest: the merge is genuinely blocked by four independent constraints (B1: `\x7fELF` and `MZ` can't share file offset 0; B2: `.ap_trampoline` LMA/VMA split doesn't survive PE/COFF conversion; B3: kernel has no `.reloc` table for UEFI image relocation; B4: GDT/CR3 handoff is moot without B1). Full diagnosis in `arch/x86/boot/efi_stub.S`'s header comment block. Two real paths out documented in `docs/BOOT.md` + `TODO.md`: PATH A (UEFI-side ELF loader baked into the stub), PATH B (bzImage-style flat-binary). Documentation-only commit closing out M16.120's "we'll merge them next" promissory note | **Diagnosis** |
| M16.125 | (TCP) Plan 9-shape TCP passive-open: LISTEN + SYN_RCVD states added to `drivers/net/tcp.ad`. New API `tcp_listen(local_port)` allocates a TCB in LISTEN state; `tcp_accept(slot, timeout)` polls for ESTABLISHED on that listener; multi-client capable (single LISTEN TCB stays in LISTEN as it accepts further inbound SYNs, with each accepted connection getting its own TCB slot). `tcp_rx` matches LISTEN TCBs by local_port before the existing remote-tuple match; fresh ISN per connection via xorshift64. | M16.126 | **UEFI direct boot SHIPPED via PATH A** — kernel actually runs end-to-end under UEFI firmware now. EFI stub uses UEFI's Simple File System Protocol to read `\hamnix-kernel.elf` from the ESP, parses ELFCLASS32 program headers, memcpy's PT_LOAD bytes from `p_offset` → `p_paddr` + zero-pads `p_memsz - p_filesz`, scans the kernel for the multiboot magic to locate the M16.126-planted Hamnix EFI handoff table (`multiboot_header+48`: exposes `_x86_start_after_loader`'s VMA + `boot_via_efi`'s physical address), patches `boot_via_efi=1`, runs the M16.120 GetMemoryMap+ExitBootServices dance, installs identity-mapped page tables + kernel GDT, far-jumps to `_x86_start_after_loader`. | M16.127 | Partition-aware block-device naming (`sd0p1`, `sd0p2`, `nvme0n1p1`, ...). `kernel/block/blk.ad::blk_register_partitions(parent_slot, parent_name)` walks `partition_for(parent_slot, idx)` from M16.121, and for each valid partition registers a sibling block device named `<parent>pN` (1-indexed per Linux convention) with a partition-aware `BlockDeviceOps` vtable: read/write offset by `partition.lba_start` and bounds-checked against `partition.lba_end - partition.lba_start`. | M16.128 | PS/2 mouse driver (`drivers/input/auxmouse.ad`). Brings up the i8042 second port via controller-command-byte RMW (enable IRQ12 bit, clear AUX-clock-disable), resets the device (0xFF → ACK 0xFA + BAT 0xAA + ID 0x00 standard 3-byte mouse), enables streaming (0xF4), wires IRQ 12 → vector 0x45 via IOAPIC pin 12. Decodes the 3-byte PS/2 protocol: byte0 always-1 resync sentinel + L/R/M buttons + X/Y sign bits + X/Y overflow drop; bytes 1-2 = 9-bit signed deltas (via `_sign_extend_9bit`); Y-flipped to screen-down convention. 64-event `MouseEvent {dx, dy, buttons}` ring buffer; `mouse_rx_pop()` accessor for future `/dev/mouse` cdev. Boot-time decoder self-test covers 7 cases (positive/negative dx, Y-flip, single+multi button, byte-0 resync after invalid byte, overflow drop+recovery). Together with atkbd (M16.75/M16.100) gives Hamnix the canonical PC-AT input surface — every desktop motherboard exposes both ports | **Done** |
| M16.129 | `/dev/random` ChaCha20 + RDRAND/RDSEED upgrade — retires the M16.95 xorshift64 placeholder. Real CSPRNG: 16-word ChaCha20 state (RFC 8439 constants `expand 32-byte k` + 256-bit key + 32-bit counter + 96-bit nonce), 20-round block function, 64-byte keystream block per counter advance. CPUID-detected RDSEED (leaf 7:0 EBX bit 18) preferred, RDRAND (leaf 1 ECX bit 30) fallback, `get_jiffies() ^ counter ^ golden-ratio` last resort. Inline-asm wrappers park CPUID/RDRAND outputs in RIP-relative module-globals; %rbx saved/restored across CPUID; 10-retry loop per Intel guidance. Rekeys every 4 KiB (64 blocks) by XOR-mixing 8 fresh hwrng words into state[4..11] + resetting the counter word. Block function verified against the RFC 8439 §2.3.2 test vector (Python port matched byte-for-byte). API unchanged — M16.95 `scripts/test_devrandom.sh` regression PASSes; new `scripts/test_devrandom_chacha.sh` reads 4 KiB into 256 entropy buckets, asserts all non-zero with max/min ratio ≤ 5x. Suitable for TLS handshakes, sshd key generation, password hashing | **Done** |

Writes return -1 (read-only). Empty ring returns 0 bytes — non-blocking poll semantics; blocking-read deferred until the syscall layer's wait-queue story lands.
